\id Kizjavka_GI_life_Anavgaj_000_metadata
\ref Recorded on 20 July 2009 in Anavgai by Natalia Aralova. 
\qu ???? Transcribed by ???? translated into Russian by ????, glossed by Brigitte Pakendorf in 2016. Funding by the Volkswagen Foundation
(DoBeS grant) and CNRS/UniversitÈ Lyon 2 (laboratoire DDL). Speaker abbreviation = GIK
\ref Galina Ivanovna Kizjavka was born in 1969, i.e. she was 39-40 at the time of recording. She has a college-level education, worked in
the reindeer herd for a long time, but then obtained a degree as a pedagogical worker. She is married to a Koryak and speaks Russian
with her husband.
